mareſchall ſeeing batterie wrought great effecte yet beſieged ſhewed countenaunce woulde yeelde luſtily purſued agreed myne ſhoulde bee made right againſt batterie wherein wrought long daunger difficultie notwithſtanding ende finiſhed well cloſed ſealed vp fire put aſſaulte giuen ruyne lefte order eſtabliſhed aſſaulte ſo euill kepte beſides souldiars wente ſo ſlackely worke maiſter campe ſlayne nomber gentleman souldiers firſt aduaunced formoſt dead earth reſt beaten backe hurte many gallaunt men euente ſhewed howe armie euill ſatiſfied full captaynes souldiers diſcontented diſobedient ſucceſſe ought hoped vnfortunate meane time mareſchall ſente declare vnto king together neceſſities armie feare leaſt woulde turne ruyne inſtance duke ferrara made cauſe french armie foſſan frenche ſtill approached meanes whereof marqueſſe fearing bee encloſed conſequently himſelfe reduce place extreame neceſſitie wrought ſo well whole infanterie gayned cony thence knowing howe returne conſtrayned leade men trauerſe mountaines gayne sea ſhoare ſaue people well hee mought difficultie wayes notwithſtanding founde ſuch loſt many people ſaued themſelues ſo wearie defeated posſible bee men armes cauallerie remayned ſtill within foſſan therefore agreed waſte ſhoulde bee made round force ſhould layed longeſt paſſages wayes none cauallerie mought eſcape time thus encloſed many fayre feates notable ſkirmiſhes vndertaken diuerſly executed namely vidaſme chartres colonell fanterie piemont danuille de terrides others ſo good watche kept alongeſt pasſages many troupe ſtoode ſeconde ſummons maieſtie swizers muſt neceſſitie ſent awaythe swizers goe piemont foretolde grewe altogether vnprofitable thorough long aboade made lion ſicke weake euill payde nowe mareſchall hauing vnderſtood vpon defeate maieſtie cauſed newe company men armes addreſſed hee greatly beſought la mothe gondrin franciſque bernardrin de pauan vicompt gourdon mought gratified offered come perſon himſelfe vnto maieſtie great neceſſitie doe ſeruice woulde bee accepted certayne dayes maieſtie perceyuing howe force remayning piemont swizers departed thence foreſeeing daunger ſome made offer vnto king himſelfe vnwitting mareſchall hee mought leuie piemont two three hundred thouſande crownes leuying three crownes vpon euery houſholder offer onely accepted without aduiſe demaunded mareſchall likewiſe preſte money deliuered vnto vpon aſſignations piemont whileſt maieſtie made difficultie heare ſuch reaſons mought bee alleadged touching impoſſibilitie ſuch leuie
